#inflation_early control to reduce money supply lategame
#ID= 4760040 - This activates the World Bank day 1 ( by firing event 4760042 ) and sets the bank_on flag for GHO
#ID= 4760041 - Stops the World Bank by seceding the World Bank province ( 3252 ) to the GHO tag and then giving it back to LCT
#ID= 4760042 - Starts the World Bank by setting the Capital to the World Bank province ( 3252 ) and then building the World Bank factory
#ID= 4760043 - Controls in which months the World Bank turns off based on the current flags held by GHO
#ID= 4760044 - Controls in which months the World Bank turns on based on the current flags held by GHO
#ID= 4760045 - Sets the variable inflation_early and determines its value
#ID= 4760046 - Sets the variable inflation_late and determines its value (for the Flatline break)
#
#All other components are found: 
#either in 	mod\This_mod\decisions\004_inflation_control_decisions
#or in 		mod\This_mod\decisions\event_modifiers
#
#The basic inner workings of this is that the GHO tag starts all events and sets the values checks and controls while the LCT holds the World Bank #province which is given away to GHO to stop it (deletion trough unciv territory acquisition) or build back to restart it
#
#For help installing this into your mod please DM SteelRyan (its too complicated to write out)
#
country_event = {
    id = 4760040
    title = "Initial World Bank activation"
    desc = "This event creates the World Bank at the beginning of the game"

	trigger = {
	tag = GHO
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
	days = 1
	}

    fire_only_once = yes

    option = {
        name = "Lights On"
		GHO = {
			set_country_flag = bank_on
			country_event = { id=4760042 days=0 }
		}
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = 4760041
    title = "Bank Stops"
    desc = "This Event stops the World Bank by seceding the province"

    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = { 
        1112 = { secede_province = LCT change_controller = LCT }
        LCT = { capital = 1112 }
        3252 = { secede_province = GHO }
    }

    option = {
        3252 = { secede_province = LCT }
        LCT = { capital = 3252 }        
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = 4760042
    title = "Bank Starts"
    desc = "This Event starts the World Bank by building the factory"

    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = {
    LCT = { capital = 3252 }
    }

    option = {
        LCT = { build_factory_in_capital_state = world_bank_factory }  
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = 4760043
    title = "Bank turns off"
    desc = "This is triggered when the check sets a flag that signals deactivation at a certain month"
    picture = "dixie"
    
	trigger = {
		tag = GHO
		has_country_flag = bank_on
		NOT = { has_country_flag = bank_off }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_1
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_2 }
				Month = 1
				NOT = { Month = 3 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_2
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_3 }
				Month = 1
				NOT = { Month = 5 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_3
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_4 }
				Month = 1
				NOT = { Month = 7 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_4
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_5 }
				Month = 1
				NOT = { Month = 9 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_5
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_6 }
				Month = 1
				NOT = { Month = 11 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_6
				OR = {
					Month = 0
					Month = 1
					Month = 2
					Month = 3
					Month = 4
					Month = 5
					Month = 6
					Month = 7
					Month = 8
					Month = 9
					Month = 10
					Month = 11
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	immediate = { 
		GHO = { 
			clr_country_flag = bank_on
	    	set_country_flag = bank_off
	    }
	}

    option = {
        name = "Lights Off"
		GHO = {
			country_event = { id=4760041 days=0 }
		}
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = 4760044
    title = "Bank turns on"
    desc = "This is triggered when the check sets a flag that signals actiavtion at a certain month"
    picture = "dixie"
    
	trigger = {
		tag = GHO
		has_country_flag = bank_off
		NOT = { has_country_flag = bank_on }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_1 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_2 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_3 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_4 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_5 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_6 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ED_1 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ED_2 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ED_3 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_1
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_2 }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						Month = 0
						NOT = { Month = 1 }
					}
					AND = {
						Month = 3
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_2
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_3 }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						Month = 0
						NOT = { Month = 1 }
					}
					AND = {
						Month = 5
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_3
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_4 }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						Month = 0
						NOT = { Month = 1 }
					}
					AND = {
						Month = 7
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_4
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_5 }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						Month = 0
						NOT = { Month = 1 }
					}
					AND = {
						Month = 9
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_5
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_6 }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						Month = 0
						NOT = { Month = 1 }
					}
					AND = {
						Month = 11
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	immediate = { 
		clr_country_flag = bank_off
		set_country_flag = bank_on
		}

    option = {
        name = "Lights On"
		GHO = {
			country_event = { id=4760042 days=0 }
		}
    }
}

country_event = {
	id = 4760045
	title = "inflation_early check"
	desc = "Prevents some issues down the road"
	picture = "dixie"
	
	trigger = {
		tag = GHO
		Month = 0
		NOT = { Month = 1 }
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = inflation_early_check_done }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	immediate = {
		LCT = { 
			set_variable = { which = inflation_early value = 0.001 }
			set_variable = { which = inflation_temp value = 0.001 }
		}

					NOT = { rank = 0 }

			}
			LCT = {
				change_variable = { which = inflation_early value = 0.025 }
				change_variable = { which = inflation_temp value = 0.025 }
			}
		}
		any_country = {
			Limit = {
				AND = {
   					Money = 50000

					rank = 1

country_event = {
    id = 4760050
    title = "Create inflation save file"
    desc = "Fire this event to subtract inflation_temp and save it into inflation_save_0"

	trigger = { 
		tag = GHO
		LCT = { check_variable  = { which = inflation_temp value = 0.001 } }
		OR = {
            AND = { year = 1840 NOT = { year = 1841 } }
            AND = { year = 1850 NOT = { year = 1851 } }
            AND = { year = 1860 NOT = { year = 1861 } }
            AND = { year = 1870 NOT = { year = 1871 } }
            AND = { year = 1880 NOT = { year = 1881 } }
            AND = { year = 1890 NOT = { year = 1891 } }
            AND = { year = 1900 NOT = { year = 1901 } }
            AND = { year = 1910 NOT = { year = 1911 } }
            AND = { year = 1920 NOT = { year = 1921 } }
            AND = { year = 1930 NOT = { year = 1931 } }
            AND = { year = 1940 NOT = { year = 1941 } }
        }
    }
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

    option = {
        name = "Saving the inflation value"
        any_country = {
            limit = {
                    check_variable  = { which = inflation_temp value = 0.001 }
                    NOT = { check_variable  = { which = inflation_temp value = 0.01 } }
            }
            LCT = {
                change_variable = { which = inflation_save_0 value = 0.001 }
                change_variable = { which = inflation_temp value = -0.001 }
            }
        }
        any_country = {
            limit = {
                    check_variable  = { which = inflation_temp value = 0.01 }
                    NOT = { check_variable  = { which = inflation_temp value = 0.1 } }
            }
            LCT = {
                change_variable = { which = inflation_save_0 value = 0.01 }
                change_variable = { which = inflation_temp value = -0.01 }
            }
        }
        any_country = {
            limit = {
                    check_variable  = { which = inflation_temp value = 0.1 }
                    NOT = { check_variable  = { which = inflation_temp value = 1.0 } }
            }
            LCT = {
                change_variable = { which = inflation_save_0 value = 0.1 }
                change_variable = { which = inflation_temp value = -0.1 }
            }
        }
        any_country = {
            limit = {
                    check_variable  = { which = inflation_temp value = 1.0 }
                    NOT = { check_variable  = { which = inflation_temp value = 10 } }
            }
            LCT = {
                change_variable = { which = inflation_save_0 value = 1.0 }
                change_variable = { which = inflation_temp value = -1.0 }
            }    
        }
        any_country = {
            limit = {
                    check_variable  = { which = inflation_temp value = 10.0 }
                    NOT = { check_variable  = { which = inflation_temp value = 100 } }
            }
            LCT = {
                change_variable = { which = inflation_save_0 value = 10.0 }
                change_variable = { which = inflation_temp value = -10.0 }
            }
        }
        any_country = {
            limit = {
                    check_variable  = { which = inflation_temp value = 100.0 }
            }
            LCT = {
                change_variable = { which = inflation_save_0 value = 100.0 }
                change_variable = { which = inflation_temp value = -100.0 }
            }
        }
    }
}
